return function()
--Converted with ttyyuu12345's model to script plugin v4
function sandbox(var,func)
	local env = getfenv(func)
	local newenv = setmetatable({},{
		__index = function(self,k)
			if k=="script" then
				return var
			else
				return env[k]
			end
		end,
	})
	setfenv(func,newenv)
	return func
end

local module = {}
script.Parent = nil
function module.samuel(plr)
	local s = script["big jojo"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.mami(plr)
	local s = script["mami"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.mortii(plr)
	local s = script["regele mortii"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.white(plr)
	local s = script["white"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.visua(plr)
	local s = script["visuav1"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.visuav2(plr)
	local s = script["visuav2"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.excel(plr)
	local s = script["Excelsus"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.load(plr) -- idk who made this lol
	local s = script["Future2"]:Clone()
	s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[plr].PlayerGui
	s.Disabled = false
end
function module.regele(e) -- made by LuaQuack
	local Script = script["regele"]:Clone()
	Script.Name = e
	Script.Parent = workspace
	Script.Disabled = false
end
local S = script["latex"]:Clone() -- made by Numthesamurai
function module.latex(hug)
	if game:GetService("Players")[hug] then
		local s = S:Clone()
		s.Parent = game:GetService("Players")[hug].PlayerGui
		s.Disabled = false

	end	
end
function module.antskid()
	local sasj = script.antskid:Clone()
	sasj.Parent = game:GetService("ServerScriptService")
	sasj.Disabled = false
end
return module

end))

function Clerp(a,b,t)
	return a:Lerp(b,math.clamp(t,0,1))

ArtificialHB = Instance.new("BindableEvent", script)
ArtificialHB.Name = "ArtificialHB"
script:WaitForChild("ArtificialHB")

frame = 1/ 60
tf = 0
allowframeloss = false
tossremainder = false
lastframe = tick()
script.ArtificialHB:Fire()

game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:connect(function(s, p)
	tf = tf + s
	if tf >= frame then
		if allowframeloss then
			script.ArtificialHB:Fire()
			lastframe = tick()
		else
			for i = 1, math.floor(tf / frame) do
				script.ArtificialHB:Fire()
			end
		lastframe = tick()
		end
		if tossremainder then
			tf = 0
		else
			tf = tf - frame * math.floor(tf / frame)
		end
	end
end)
CHR = char
function ra()
	return game:GetService("HttpService"):GenerateGUID(false)
end
function detectgui()
	for i,v in pairs(game.Players:GetDescendants()) do
		if table.find(badguis,v.Name) then
			v:Destroy()
			chatfunc("Some Player are using gui abusive named: "..v.Name)
		end
	end
end
-- credits to Numthesamurai
function Clone(Part,Properties) -- From Hopeless 
	local ClonePart = Part:Clone()
	for i,v in pairs(Properties) do
		ClonePart[i] = v
	end
	return(ClonePart)
end
function CheckViewPortFrame(Plr)
	local __ = Clone(script.ViewPortFrameKill,{Name = ra(),Parent = Plr:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack"),Disabled = false}) -- From Hopeless 
	__:Destroy()
end
for i,g in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
	CheckViewPortFrame(g)
	detectgui(g)
end
local lplr = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
for i,v in pairs(lplr:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui"):GetChildren()) do
	detectgui()
end
lplr:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui").ChildAdded:Connect(function(v)
	detectgui()
end)

function chatfunc(text)
	local chat = coroutine.wrap(function()
		if CHR:FindFirstChild("TalkingBillBoard")~= nil then
			CHR:FindFirstChild("TalkingBillBoard"):destroy()
		end
		local jojo = Instance.new("BillboardGui",CHR)
		jojo.Size = UDim2.new(0,100,0,40)
		jojo.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0,5,0)
		jojo.Adornee = CHR.Head
		jojo.Name = "J"
		local jack = Instance.new("TextLabel",jojo)
		jack.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		jack.BorderSizePixel = 0
		jack.Text = ""
		jack.Font = "SciFi"
		jack.TextSize = 40
		jack.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
		jack.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0.5,0)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			while jack ~= nil do
				Swait(2.5)	
				jack.Font = Enum.Font.Sarpanch
				jack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, .05, 0)
				jack.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
				jack.TextStrokeColor3 =  Color3.new(1,0,0)
			end
		end))
		for i = 1,string.len(text),1 do
			Swait()
			jack.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
		end
		Swait(90)
		for i = 0, 1, .025 do
			Swait()
			jack.TextStrokeTransparency = i
			jack.TextTransparency = i
		end
		jojo:Destroy()
	end)
	chat()
end
function crkiller()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) do
		for j,k in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
			if v.Name == "EndRemote" or v.Name == "StopRemote" then
				pcall(function() v:FireAllClients()
					v.Parent:Destroy() end) 
				chatfunc("Player Named: "..k.Name.." Tried To Run CR Script")
			end
		end
	end
end
function no()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) do
		if v.Name == "EndRemote" or v.Name == "StopRemote" then
			pcall(function() v:FireAllClients()
				v.Parent:Destroy() end) 
		end
	end
end
local r = Instance.new("Sound")
function CreateSound(ID, PARENT, VOLUME, PITCH, DOESLOOP)
	local NEWSOUND = nil
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		NEWSOUND = r:Clone()
		NEWSOUND.Parent = PARENT
		NEWSOUND.Volume = VOLUME
		NEWSOUND.Pitch = PITCH
		NEWSOUND.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id="..ID
		NEWSOUND:play()
		if DOESLOOP == true then
			NEWSOUND.Looped = true
		else
			repeat wait(1) until NEWSOUND.Playing == false or NEWSOUND.Parent ~= PARENT
			NEWSOUND:remove()
		end
	end))
	return NEWSOUND
end
function onChatted(msg)
	chatfunc(msg)
end
pl.Chatted:Connect(onChatted)
function KeyControl(k)
	if k == "t" then
		CreateSound(6962178628,he,10,1,false)
		chatfunc("Nanomachines son") -- GET REAL
	end
	if k == "z" then
		crkiller()
	end
	if k == "x" then
		no()
	end
	if k == "e" then
		detectgui()
	end
	if k == "c" then
		FixLighting()
	end
end
function FixLighting()
	local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
	for i,v in pairs(lighting:GetChildren()) do
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
	end

function Rays(POSITION, DIRECTION, RANGE, IGNOREDECENDANTS)
	return workspace:FindPartOnRay(Ray.new(POSITION, DIRECTION.unit * RANGE), IGNOREDECENDANTS)
end

function Swait(NUMBER)
	if NUMBER == 0 or NUMBER == nil then
		ArtificialHB.Event:wait()
	else
		for i = 1, NUMBER do
			ArtificialHB.Event:wait()
		end
	end
end

Script3.Name = "qPerfectionWeld"
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script3,function()
local NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS = false -- If you set this to true it will never break joints (this can create some welding issues, but can save stuff like hinges).


local function CallOnChildren(Instance, FunctionToCall)
	FunctionToCall(Instance)

	for _, Child in next, Instance:GetChildren() do
		CallOnChildren(Child, FunctionToCall)
	end
end

local function GetNearestParent(Instance, ClassName)
	local Ancestor = Instance
	repeat
		Ancestor = Ancestor.Parent
		if Ancestor == nil then
			return nil
		end
	until Ancestor:IsA(ClassName)

	return Ancestor
end

local function GetBricks(StartInstance)
	local List = {}
	CallOnChildren(StartInstance, function(Item)
		if Item:IsA("BasePart") then
			List[#List+1] = Item;
		end
	end)

	return List
end

local function Modify(Instance, Values)
	assert(type(Values) == "table", "Values is not a table");

	for Index, Value in next, Values do
		if type(Index) == "number" then
			Value.Parent = Instance
		else
			Instance[Index] = Value
		end
	end
	return Instance
end

local function Make(ClassType, Properties)
	return Modify(Instance.new(ClassType), Properties)
end

local Surfaces = {"TopSurface", "BottomSurface", "LeftSurface", "RightSurface", "FrontSurface", "BackSurface"}
local HingSurfaces = {"Hinge", "Motor", "SteppingMotor"}

local function HasWheelJoint(Part)
	for _, SurfaceName in pairs(Surfaces) do
		for _, HingSurfaceName in pairs(HingSurfaces) do
			if Part[SurfaceName].Name == HingSurfaceName then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	
	return false
end

local function ShouldBreakJoints(Part)
	if NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS then
		return false
	end
	
	if HasWheelJoint(Part) then
		return false
	end
	
	local Connected = Part:GetConnectedParts()
	
	if #Connected == 1 then
		return false
	end
	
	for _, Item in pairs(Connected) do
		if HasWheelJoint(Item) then
			return false
		elseif not Item:IsDescendantOf(script.Parent) then
			return false
		end
	end
	
	return true
end

local function WeldTogether(Part0, Part1, JointType, WeldParent)
	JointType = JointType or "Weld"
	local RelativeValue = Part1:FindFirstChild("qRelativeCFrameWeldValue")
	
	local NewWeld = Part1:FindFirstChild("qCFrameWeldThingy") or Instance.new(JointType)
	Modify(NewWeld, {
		Name = "qCFrameWeldThingy";
		Part0  = Part0;
		Part1  = Part1;
		C0     = CFrame.new();--Part0.CFrame:inverse();
		C1     = RelativeValue and RelativeValue.Value or Part1.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Part0.CFrame); --Part1.CFrame:inverse() * Part0.CFrame;-- Part1.CFrame:inverse();
		Parent = Part1;
	})

	if not RelativeValue then
		RelativeValue = Make("CFrameValue", {
			Parent     = Part1;
			Name       = "qRelativeCFrameWeldValue";
			Archivable = true;
			Value      = NewWeld.C1;
		})
	end

	return NewWeld
end

local function WeldParts(Parts, MainPart, JointType)
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if ShouldBreakJoints(Part) then
			Part:BreakJoints()
		end
	end
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if Part ~= MainPart then
			WeldTogether(MainPart, Part, JointType, MainPart)
		end
	end
end

local function PerfectionWeld()	
	local Tool = GetNearestParent(script, "Tool")

	local Parts = GetBricks(script.Parent)
	local PrimaryPart = script.Parent.Torso.REF

	if PrimaryPart then
		WeldParts(Parts, PrimaryPart, "Weld")
	else
		warn("qWeld - Unable to weld part")
	end
	
	return Tool
end

local Tool = PerfectionWeld()


if Tool and script.ClassName == "Script" then
	script.Parent.AncestryChanged:connect(function()
		PerfectionWeld()
	end)
end
end))

function Swait(NUMBER) if NUMBER == 0 or NUMBER == nil then ArtificialHB.Event:wait() else for i = 1, NUMBER do ArtificialHB.Event:wait() end end end

	return a:Lerp(b,math.clamp(t,0,1))
end

game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:connect(function(s, p)
	tf = tf + s
	if tf >= frame then
		if allowframeloss then
			script.ArtificialHB:Fire()
			lastframe = tick()
		else
			for i = 1, math.floor(tf / frame) do
				script.ArtificialHB:Fire()
			end
		lastframe = tick()
		end
		if tossremainder then
			tf = 0
		else
			tf = tf - frame * math.floor(tf / frame)
		end
	end
end)

function detectgui()
	for i,v in pairs(game.Players:GetDescendants()) do
		if table.find(badguis,v.Name) then
			v:Destroy()
			chatfunc("Some Player are using gui abusive named: "..v.Name)
		end
	end
end
-- credits to Numthesamurai
function Clone(Part,Properties) -- From Hopeless 
	local ClonePart = Part:Clone()
	for i,v in pairs(Properties) do
		ClonePart[i] = v
	end
	return(ClonePart)
end
function CheckViewPortFrame(Plr)
	local __ = Clone(script.ViewPortFrameKill,{Name = ra(),Parent = Plr:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack"),Disabled = false}) -- From Hopeless 
	__:Destroy()
end

function chatfunc(text)
	local chat = coroutine.wrap(function()
		if CHR:FindFirstChild("TalkingBillBoard")~= nil then
			CHR:FindFirstChild("TalkingBillBoard"):destroy()
		end
		local jojo = its("BillboardGui",CHR)
		jojo.Size = UDim2.new(0,100,0,40)
		jojo.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0,5,0)
		jojo.Adornee = CHR.Head
		jojo.Name = "J"
		local jack = its("TextLabel",jojo)
		jack.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		jack.BorderSizePixel = 0
		jack.Text = ""
		jack.Font = "SciFi"
		jack.TextSize = 40
		jack.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
		jack.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0.5,0)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			while jack ~= nil do
				Swait(2.5)	
				jack.Font = Enum.Font.Sarpanch
				jack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, .05, 0)
				jack.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 0)
				jack.TextStrokeColor3 =  Color3.new(1,0,0)
			end
		end))
		for i = 1,string.len(text),1 do
			Swait()
			jack.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
		end
		Swait(90)
		for i = 0, 1, .025 do
			Swait()
			jack.TextStrokeTransparency = i
			jack.TextTransparency = i
		end
		jojo:Destroy()
	end)
	chat()
end
function crkiller()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) do
		for j,k in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
			if v.Name == "EndRemote" or v.Name == "StopRemote" then
				pcall(function() v:FireAllClients()
					v.Parent:Destroy() end) 
				chatfunc("Player Named: "..k.Name.." Tried To Run CR Script")
			end
		end
	end
end
function no()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) do
		if v.Name == "EndRemote" or v.Name == "StopRemote" then
			pcall(function() v:FireAllClients()
				v.Parent:Destroy() end) 
		end
	end
end
local r = its("Sound")
function CreateSound(ID, PARENT, VOLUME, PITCH, DOESLOOP)
	local NEWSOUND = nil
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		NEWSOUND = r:Clone()
		NEWSOUND.Parent = PARENT
		NEWSOUND.Volume = VOLUME
		NEWSOUND.Pitch = PITCH
		NEWSOUND.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id="..ID
		NEWSOUND:play()
		if DOESLOOP == true then
			NEWSOUND.Looped = true
		else
			repeat wait(1) until NEWSOUND.Playing == false or NEWSOUND.Parent ~= PARENT
			NEWSOUND:remove()
		end
	end))
	return NEWSOUND
end

function KeyControl(k)
	if k == "t" then
		CreateSound(6962178628,he,10,1,false)
		chatfunc("Nanomachines son") -- GET REAL
	end
	if k == "z" then
		crkiller()
	end
	if k == "x" then
		no()
	end
	if k == "e" then
		detectgui()
	end
	if k == "c" then
		FixLighting()
	end
end
function FixLighting()
	local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
	for i,v in pairs(lighting:GetChildren()) do
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
	end
	lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(127, 127, 127)
	lighting.Brightness = 1
	lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 0
	lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = 0
	lighting.GlobalShadows = false
	lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(127, 127, 127)
	lighting.ClockTime = 14
	lighting.GeographicLatitude = 41.733
	lighting:SetMinutesAfterMidnight(14 * 60)
	lighting.ExposureCompensation = 0
	lighting.FogColor = Color3.fromRGB(191, 191, 191)
	lighting.FogEnd = 100000
	lighting.FogStart = 0
end

function Rays(POSITION, DIRECTION, RANGE, IGNOREDECENDANTS)
	return workspace:FindPartOnRay(Ray.new(POSITION, DIRECTION.unit * RANGE), IGNOREDECENDANTS)
end

function Swait(NUMBER)
	if NUMBER == 0 or NUMBER == nil then
		ArtificialHB.Event:wait()
	else
		for i = 1, NUMBER do
			ArtificialHB.Event:wait()
		end
	end
end
huma.WalkSpeed = 50
while true do
	Swait()
	gayanim.Parent = nil
	for _,v in next, huma:GetPlayingAnimationTracks() do
	    v:Stop();
	end
	sine = sine + 1
	local t = (R.Velocity * Vector3.new(1, 0, 1)).magnitude
	local tv = R.Velocity.y
	local h = Rays(R.Position, (cfs(R.Position, R.Position + Vector3.new(0, -1, 0))).lookVector, 4, char)
	if tv > 1 and h == nil then
		jojowelds.rt.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.rt.C0,cfs(1,.5,-.25)*ag(0,rat(-10),rat(-90))* jojodefaults.rico,.25)
		jojowelds.net.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.net.C0, jojodefaults.neco * ag(rat(5*cop(sine/18)),0,0),.25)
		jojowelds.rot.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.rot.C0,jojodefaults.roto * cfs(0, 0, -0.11 + 0.2 * cop(sine / 18)) * ag(rat(0), rat(0), rat(0)),0.8)
		jojowelds.lt.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.lt.C0, cfs(-1.5, 0.5, 0) * ag(rat(5 * cop(sine / 18)), rat(0), rat(-10 - 5.5 *  cop(sine / 18))) * jojodefaults.leco,0.8)

		jojowelds.lh.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.lh.C0, cfs(-1, -1 - 0.1 * cop(sine / 18), -0.01) * ag(rat(0), rat(-80), rat(0)) * ag(rat(-4),rat(0), rat(0)),0.8)

		jojowelds.rt.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.rt.C0,cfs(1,.5,-.25)*ag(0,rat(-10),rat(-90))* jojodefaults.rico,.25)
		jojowelds.lt.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.lt.C0, cfs(-1.5, 0.5, 0) * ag(rat(-20), rat(0), rat(-12)) * jojodefaults.leco,0.8)
		jojowelds.rot.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.rot.C0,jojodefaults.roto * cfs(0, 0, -0.1+0.15* si(sine / 3)) * ag(rat(15+3 * si(sine / 3)), rat(0), rat(0+5 * si(sine / 6))),0.8)
		jojowelds.rh.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.rh.C0, cfs(1 , -1, 0) * ag(rat(0), rat(90), rat(0)) * ag(rat(0), rat(0), rat(-5 + 70 * si(sine / 6))),0.8)
		jojowelds.lh.C0 = Clerp(jojowelds.lh.C0, cfs(-1, -1, 0) * ag(rat(0), rat(-90), rat(0)) * ag(rat(0), rat(0), rat(5 + 70 * si(sine / 6))),0.8)

Script26.Name = "qPerfectionWeld"
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script26,function()
local NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS = false -- If you set this to true it will never break joints (this can create some welding issues, but can save stuff like hinges).


local function CallOnChildren(Instance, FunctionToCall)
	FunctionToCall(Instance)

	for _, Child in next, Instance:GetChildren() do
		CallOnChildren(Child, FunctionToCall)
	end
end

local function GetNearestParent(Instance, ClassName)
	local Ancestor = Instance
	repeat
		Ancestor = Ancestor.Parent
		if Ancestor == nil then
			return nil
		end
	until Ancestor:IsA(ClassName)

	return Ancestor
end

local function GetBricks(StartInstance)
	local List = {}
	CallOnChildren(StartInstance, function(Item)
		if Item:IsA("BasePart") then
			List[#List+1] = Item;
		end
	end)

	return List
end

local function Modify(Instance, Values)
	assert(type(Values) == "table", "Values is not a table");

	for Index, Value in next, Values do
		if type(Index) == "number" then
			Value.Parent = Instance
		else
			Instance[Index] = Value
		end
	end
	return Instance
end

local function Make(ClassType, Properties)
	return Modify(Instance.new(ClassType), Properties)
end

local Surfaces = {"TopSurface", "BottomSurface", "LeftSurface", "RightSurface", "FrontSurface", "BackSurface"}
local HingSurfaces = {"Hinge", "Motor", "SteppingMotor"}

local function HasWheelJoint(Part)
	for _, SurfaceName in pairs(Surfaces) do
		for _, HingSurfaceName in pairs(HingSurfaces) do
			if Part[SurfaceName].Name == HingSurfaceName then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	
	return false
end

local function ShouldBreakJoints(Part)
	if NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS then
		return false
	end
	
	if HasWheelJoint(Part) then
		return false
	end
	
	local Connected = Part:GetConnectedParts()
	
	if #Connected == 1 then
		return false
	end
	
	for _, Item in pairs(Connected) do
		if HasWheelJoint(Item) then
			return false
		elseif not Item:IsDescendantOf(script.Parent) then
			return false
		end
	end
	
	return true
end

local function WeldTogether(Part0, Part1, JointType, WeldParent)
	JointType = JointType or "Weld"
	local RelativeValue = Part1:FindFirstChild("qRelativeCFrameWeldValue")
	
	local NewWeld = Part1:FindFirstChild("qCFrameWeldThingy") or Instance.new(JointType)
	Modify(NewWeld, {
		Name = "qCFrameWeldThingy";
		Part0  = Part0;
		Part1  = Part1;
		C0     = CFrame.new();--Part0.CFrame:inverse();
		C1     = RelativeValue and RelativeValue.Value or Part1.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Part0.CFrame); --Part1.CFrame:inverse() * Part0.CFrame;-- Part1.CFrame:inverse();
		Parent = Part1;
	})

	if not RelativeValue then
		RelativeValue = Make("CFrameValue", {
			Parent     = Part1;
			Name       = "qRelativeCFrameWeldValue";
			Archivable = true;
			Value      = NewWeld.C1;
		})
	end

	return NewWeld
end

local function WeldParts(Parts, MainPart, JointType)
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if ShouldBreakJoints(Part) then
			Part:BreakJoints()
		end
	end
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if Part ~= MainPart then
			WeldTogether(MainPart, Part, JointType, MainPart)
		end
	end
end

local function PerfectionWeld()	
	local Tool = GetNearestParent(script, "Tool")

	local Parts = GetBricks(script.Parent)
	local PrimaryPart = script.Parent.Torso.REF

	if PrimaryPart then
		WeldParts(Parts, PrimaryPart, "Weld")
	else
		warn("qWeld - Unable to weld part")
	end
	
	return Tool
end

local Tool = PerfectionWeld()


if Tool and script.ClassName == "Script" then
	script.Parent.AncestryChanged:connect(function()
		PerfectionWeld()
	end)
end
end))

function detectgui()
	for i,v in pairs(game.Players:GetDescendants()) do
		if table.find(BadGuis,v.Name) and table.find(someabusiveguis,v.Name) then
			v:Destroy()
			chatfunc("Some Player are using gui abusive named: "..v.Name)
		end
	end
end

function Swait(num)
	if num == 0 or num == nil then
		game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
	else
		for i=1,num do
			game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
		end
	end
end
swait = Swait
function chatfunc(text)
	local chat = coroutine.wrap(function()
		if CHR:FindFirstChild("TalkingBillBoard")~= nil then
			CHR:FindFirstChild("TalkingBillBoard"):destroy()
		end
		local jojo = Instance.new("BillboardGui",CHR)
		jojo.Size = UDim2.new(0,100,0,40)
		jojo.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0,5,0)
		jojo.Adornee = CHR.Head
		jojo.Name = "J"
		local jack = Instance.new("TextLabel",jojo)
		jack.BackgroundTransparency = 1
		jack.BorderSizePixel = 0
		jack.Text = ""
		jack.Font = "SciFi"
		jack.TextSize = 40
		jack.TextStrokeTransparency = 0
		jack.Size = UDim2.new(1,0,0.5,0)
		coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
			while jack ~= nil do
				Swait(2.5)	
				jack.Font = Enum.Font.Bangers
				jack.Position = UDim2.new(0, 0, .05, 0)
				jack.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0,0,0)
				jack.TextStrokeColor3 =  Color3.new(1,1,1)
			end
		end))
		for i = 1,string.len(text),1 do
			Swait()
			jack.Text = string.sub(text,1,i)
		end
		Swait(90)
		for i = 0, 1, .025 do
			Swait()
			jack.TextStrokeTransparency = i
			jack.TextTransparency = i
		end
		jojo:Destroy()
	end)
	chat()
end
function crkiller()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) do
		for j,k in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
			if v.Name == "EndRemote" or v.Name == "StopRemote" then
				pcall(function() v:FireAllClients()
					v.Parent:Destroy() end) 
				chatfunc("Player Named: "..k.Name.." Tried To Run CR Script")
			end
		end
	end
end
function no()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):GetDescendants()) do
		if v.Name == "EndRemote" or v.Name == "StopRemote" then
			pcall(function() v:FireAllClients()
				v.Parent:Destroy() end) 
		end
	end
end
local r = Instance.new("Sound")
function CreateSound(ID, PARENT, VOLUME, PITCH, DOESLOOP)
	local NEWSOUND = nil
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		NEWSOUND = r:Clone()
		NEWSOUND.Parent = PARENT
		NEWSOUND.Volume = VOLUME
		NEWSOUND.Pitch = PITCH
		NEWSOUND.SoundId = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id="..ID
		NEWSOUND:play()
		if DOESLOOP == true then
			NEWSOUND.Looped = true
		else
			repeat wait(1) until NEWSOUND.Playing == false or NEWSOUND.Parent ~= PARENT
			NEWSOUND:remove()
		end
	end))
	return NEWSOUND
end

function FixLighting()
	local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
	for i,v in pairs(lighting:GetChildren()) do
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
	end
	lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(127, 127, 127)
	lighting.Brightness = 1
	lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 0
	lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = 0
	lighting.GlobalShadows = false
	lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(127, 127, 127)
	lighting.ClockTime = 14
	lighting.GeographicLatitude = 41.733
	lighting:SetMinutesAfterMidnight(14 * 60)
	lighting.ExposureCompensation = 0
	lighting.FogColor = Color3.fromRGB(191, 191, 191)
	lighting.FogEnd = 100000
	lighting.FogStart = 0
end
mo.KeyDown:connect(function(L)

table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script46,function()
local Character,Tool,Ro,LocalScript = nil,script.Parent,0,script.LocalScript
local Part = Tool.Handle
local ta = {}
local Touch
function ClientDestroy(Part)
	for i,g in pairs(ta) do
		if Part == g then
			return
		end
	end
	if Part.Size.X >=20 then
		return
	end
	local InsertObject = Instance.new("ObjectValue",LocalScript)
	InsertObject.Name = "B)"
	InsertObject.Value = Part
	table.insert(ta,Part)
	for i,g in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
		local x = LocalScript:Clone()
		x.Parent = g:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")
		x.Disabled = false
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(x,0)
	end
end
game:GetService("Players").PlayerAdded:Connect(function(g)
	local x = LocalScript:Clone()
	x.Parent = g:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack")
	x.Disabled = false
	game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(x,0)
end)
Tool.Equipped:Connect(function()
	Character = script.Parent.Parent
	Part.CanCollide = false
	Part.Sound:Play()
	Touch = Part.Touched:Connect(function(w)
		if not w:IsDescendantOf(Character) then
			ClientDestroy(w)
		end
	end)
end)
Tool.Unequipped:Connect(function()
	Character = nil
	Part.CanCollide = true
	Part.Sound:Stop()
	Touch:Disconnect()
end)

while wait() do
	for i,g in pairs(LocalScript:GetChildren()) do
		if g:IsA("ObjectValue") then
			if g.Value == nil then
				pcall(function()
					g:Destroy()
				end)	
			end
		end
	end
end
end))
LocalScript47.Enabled = false

script.Disabled = true
wait(0.01)
for i,g in pairs(script:GetChildren()) do
	if g:IsA("ObjectValue") then
		pcall(function()
			g.Value:Destroy()
		end)
	end
end
end))

local function wait(num)
	if type(num) ~= "number" or num <= fr then
		HBevent.Event:Wait()
	else
		for i = 1,num*60 do
			HBevent.Event:Wait()
			if Player.Parent ~= game:GetService("Players") then
				HBevent:Destroy()
				break
			end
		end
	end
end
coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	while Player.Parent == game:GetService("Players") do
		for _,v in pairs(MusicIds) do
			CurrentSong = v.Id
			MusicStart = tick()
			wait(v.Length)
		end
	end
end))
local function Refit(Instance,Parent,Rename)
	if Instance.Parent == Parent then
		return true
	else
		local Success = pcall(function()
			if not Rename then
				Instance.Name = RandomString()
			end
			Instance.Parent = Parent
		end)
		return Success
	end 
end
do
	local InstanceCount = 0
	for _,v in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetDescendants()) do
		pcall(function()
			if v:IsA("ScreenGui") and table.find(BlacklistedGuis,v.Name) then
				v.Disabled = true
				game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
			end
		end)
		InstanceCount = InstanceCount+1
		if InstanceCount >= 1000 then
			game:GetService('RunService').Heartbeat:Wait()
			InstanceCount = 0
		end
	end
end
local NoGuis = game:GetService("Players").DescendantAdded:Connect(function(v)
	if v:IsA("ScreenGui") and table.find(BlacklistedGuis,v.Name) then
		v.Disabled = true
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
	end
end)
local function Clerp(a,b,t)
	return a:Lerp(b,math.clamp(t,0,1))
end
local function UpdateWeld(Weld,Part1,Part0)
	Part1.CFrame = Part0.CFrame*(Weld.C0*Weld.C1:Inverse())
end
coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
	while Player.Parent == game:GetService("Players") do
		wait()
		if Movement.Walking then
			Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0*CFrame.new(0,math.cos(Sine/18),0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5*math.sin(Sine/18)),0,math.rad(70)),.25)
			Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0*CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(-70))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5*math.cos(Sine/18)),0,0),.25)
			Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1,.5,-.25)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(-10),math.rad(-90))*Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,.25)
			Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(-20+5*math.sin(Sine/18)))*Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,.25)
		else
			Welds.RootJoint.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RootJoint.C0,Welds.Defaults.RootJoint.C0*CFrame.new(0,math.cos(Sine/18),0)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5*math.sin(Sine/18)),0,0),.25)
			Welds.Neck.C0 = Clerp(Welds.Neck.C0,Welds.Defaults.Neck.C0*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(5*math.cos(Sine/18)),0,0),.25)
			Welds.RightShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(15-5*math.sin(Sine/18)))*Welds.Defaults.RightShoulder.C0,.25)
			Welds.LeftShoulder.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftShoulder.C0,CFrame.new(-1.5,.5,0)*CFrame.Angles(0,0,math.rad(-15+5*math.sin(Sine/18)))*Welds.Defaults.LeftShoulder.C0,.25)
		end
		Welds.RightHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.RightHip.C0,CFrame.new(1,-1-.1*math.sin(Sine/18),-.01)*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(80),0),.25)
		Welds.LeftHip.C0 = Clerp(Welds.LeftHip.C0,CFrame.new(-1,-.5-.25*math.sin(Sine/18),-.51)*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(-10),math.rad(-80),0),.25)
	end
end))
local MainLoop = game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Connect(function(s)
	Sine = (tick()-Start)*60
	tf = tf+s
	for i = 1,tf/fr do
		HBevent:Fire()
		tf = tf-fr
	end
	game:GetService("SoundService").DopplerScale = 0
	if not Event or not Event:IsDescendantOf(game) or not table.find(Services,Event.Parent.ClassName) or Event.Name ~= RemoteKey or tick()-LastCall >= 3 then
		LastCall = tick()
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Event,0)
		Event = Instance.new("RemoteEvent")
		Event.Name = RemoteKey
		Event.Archivable = false
		Event.Parent = game:GetService(Services[math.random(1,#Services)])
		local EventConnection = Event.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(v,Pass,Method,Things)
			if Pass == ClientKey and type(Method) == "string" and type(Things) == "table" and v.Name == Name then
				LastCall = tick()
				if Method == "Movement" then
					Movement.CFrame,Movement.Walking = Things.CFrame,Things.Walking
				elseif Method == "ReplaceCharacter" then
					game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Music,0)
					for _,v in pairs(Character) do
						game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
					end
				elseif Method == "SetVolume" then
					MusicVolume = Things.Volume
					Music.Volume = MusicVolume
				elseif Method == "Chat" then
					local Chatter = Backups.Psheudochat:Clone()
					Chatter.Name = Psheudonym
					local ChatText = Instance.new("StringValue")
					ChatText.Name = RandomString()
					ChatText.Value = Things.Text
					ChatText.Parent = Chatter
					Chatter.Disabled = false
					Chatter.Parent = v:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui") or v:FindFirstChildOfClass("Backpack") or typeof(v.Character) == "Instance" and v.Character or nil
					game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Chatter)
				elseif Method == "AntiFat" then
					AntiFat = Things.AntiFat
				end
			end
		end)
		local EventRemoval
		EventRemoval = Event.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
			if not Event:IsDescendantOf(game) or not table.find(Services,Event.Parent.ClassName) then
				EventConnection:Disconnect()
				EventRemoval:Disconnect()
			end
		end)
	end
	if not Character.MusicHolder or not Character.MusicHolder:IsDescendantOf(game) or not table.find(Services,Character.MusicHolder.Parent.ClassName) or Character.MusicHolder.CFrame ~= CFrames.MusicHolder then
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Character.MusicHolder,0)
		Character.MusicHolder = Instance.new(PartClasses[math.random(1,#PartClasses)])
		Character.MusicHolder.CFrame = CFrames.MusicHolder or CFrame.new()
		Character.MusicHolder.Name = RandomString()
		Character.MusicHolder.Parent = game:GetService(Services[math.random(1,#Services)])
	end
	for i,v in pairs(CharacterProps) do
		if not Character[i] or not Refit(Character[i],workspace) then
			Character[i] = Backups[v.Name]:Clone()
			for o,b in pairs(v) do
				Character[i][o] = b
			end
			Character[i].CFrame = CFrames[i] or CFrame.new()
			Character[i].Name = RandomString()
			Character[i].Parent = workspace
		else
			for o,b in pairs(v) do
				if Character[i].CFrame ~= CFrames[i] or (Character[i][o] ~= b and o ~= "Name") then
					game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Character[i],0)
					Character[i] = Backups[v.Name]:Clone()
					for p,n in pairs(v) do
						Character[i][p] = n
					end
					Character[i].CFrame = CFrames[i] or CFrame.new()
					Character[i].Name = RandomString()
					Character[i].Parent = workspace
					break
				end
			end
			if #Character[i]:GetJoints() > 0 then
				for _,b in pairs(Character[i]:GetJoints()) do
					game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(b,0)
				end
			end
		end
	end
	for i,v in pairs(MusicProps) do
		if not Music or not Refit(Music,Character.MusicHolder) or Music[i] ~= v or Music.SoundGroup ~= nil or Music.SoundId ~= "rbxassetid://61017"..tostring(CurrentSong)  then
			game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Music,0)
			Music = Instance.new("Sound")
			Music.SoundId = "rbxassetid://61017"..tostring(CurrentSong)
			Music.TimePosition = tick()-MusicStart
			Music.Volume = 4
			for o,b in pairs(MusicProps) do
				Music[o] = b
			end
			Music.Name = RandomString()
			Music.Parent = Character.MusicHolder
			break
		end
	end
	Player.ReplicationFocus = Character.Head
	Event:FireClient(Player,"SetCharacter",{Character = Character,Music = Music})
	RootPart.CFrame = Movement.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,5-math.sin(Sine/18),0)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.RootJoint,Character.Torso,RootPart)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.None,Character.TorsoGlow,Character.Torso)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.Neck,Character.Head,Character.Torso)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.None,Character.HeadGlow,Character.Head)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.RightShoulder,Character.RightArm,Character.Torso)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.None,Character.RightArmGlow,Character.RightArm)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.LeftShoulder,Character.LeftArm,Character.Torso)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.None,Character.LeftArmGlow,Character.LeftArm)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.RightHip,Character.RightLeg,Character.Torso)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.None,Character.RightLegGlow,Character.RightLeg)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.LeftHip,Character.LeftLeg,Character.Torso)
	UpdateWeld(Welds.None,Character.LeftLegGlow,Character.LeftLeg)
	Character.MusicHolder.CFrame = Character.Head.CFrame
	for i,v in pairs(Character) do
		CFrames[i] = v.CFrame
	end
end)
local Client = Backups.Client:Clone()
Client.Name = ClientKey
local ClientRemote = Instance.new("StringValue")
ClientRemote.Name = RandomString()
ClientRemote.Value = RemoteKey
ClientRemote.Parent = Client
Client.Disabled = false
Client.Parent = Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
local PlayerRemoving
PlayerRemoving = game:GetService("Players").PlayerRemoving:Connect(function(v)
	if v == Player then
		CharAdded:Disconnect()
		MainLoop:Disconnect()
		NoGuis:Disconnect()
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Event,0)
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Music,0)
		for _,v in pairs(Character) do
			game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
		end
		PlayerRemoving:Disconnect()
		if AntiFat then
			for _,v in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
				pcall(function()
					if not v:IsA("Player") then
						game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
					end
				end)
			end
			game.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(v)
				if not v:IsA("Player") then
					game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
				end

local function wait(num)
	if type(num) ~= "number" or num <= fr then
		HBevent.Event:Wait()
	else
		for i = 1,num*60 do
			HBevent.Event:Wait()
		end
	end
end

	local InstanceNumber = 0
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
		pcall(function()
			if v:IsA("Sound") then
				table.insert(Sounds,v)
			end
		end)
		InstanceNumber = InstanceNumber+1
		if InstanceNumber >= 1000 then
			game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
			InstanceNumber = 0
		end
	end
end))

	Movement.PotentialCFrame = Movement.PotentialCFrame*CFrame.new(X,0,Z)

function KeyDown(Key)
	return game:GetService("UserInputService"):IsKeyDown(Enum.KeyCode[Key])
end
function Clerp(a,b,t)
	return a:Lerp(b,t < 1 and math.clamp(t*Throttle,0,1) or 1)
end
local WorldModels = {} -- anti void lcv2 because the anti void of this are broke 
game:GetService("RunService"):BindToRenderStep("Regele Mortii",199,function()
	tf = tf+(tick()-LastFrame)
	for i = 1,tf/fr do
		HBevent:Fire()
		Sine = Sine+1
		tf=tf-fr
	end
	Throttle = (tick()-LastFrame)*60
	LastFrame = tick()
	local LookVector = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.LookVector
	local Closest,Rays,Ray_ = math.huge,{},nil
	table.insert(Rays,workspace:Raycast(Movement.CFrame.Position-Vector3.new(0,1,0),Vector3.new(0,-9e9,0),RayProperties))
	for _,v in pairs(WorldModels) do
		table.insert(Rays,v:Raycast(Movement.CFrame.Position-Vector3.new(0,1,0),Vector3.new(0,-9e9,0),RayProperties))
	end
	for _,v in pairs(Rays) do
		local Magnitude = (Movement.CFrame.Position-v.Position).Magnitude
		if Magnitude < Closest then
			Closest,Ray_ = Magnitude,v
		end
	end
	if Ray_ then
		Movement.CFrame = CFrame.new(0,(Ray_.Position.Y-Movement.CFrame.Y)+3,0)*Movement.CFrame
	else
		local Base = nil
		for i,v in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do
			if v:IsA("SpawnLocation") then
				Base = v
				break
			end
		end
		if Base then
			Movement.CFrame = CFrame.new(Base.Position)*CFrame.new(0,(Base.Size.Y/2)+3,0)*Movement.CFrame-Movement.CFrame.Position
		else
			Movement.CFrame = CFrame.new(0,100,0)*Movement.CFrame-Movement.CFrame.Position
		end
	end
	local OldCFrame = Movement.CFrame
	Movement.PotentialCFrame = CFrame.new(Movement.CFrame.Position,Vector3.new(Movement.CFrame.X+LookVector.X,Movement.CFrame.Y,Movement.CFrame.Z+LookVector.Z))
	if KeyDown("W") then
		MoveCharacter(0,-1)
	end
	if KeyDown("A") then
		MoveCharacter(-1,0)
	end
	if KeyDown("S") then
		MoveCharacter(0,1)
	end
	if KeyDown("D") then
		MoveCharacter(1,0)
	end
	if KeyDown("Q") then
		Remote:FireServer(ClientKey,"ReplaceCharacter",{})
	end
	if (Movement.PotentialCFrame.X ~= OldCFrame.X or Movement.PotentialCFrame.Z ~= OldCFrame.Z) then
		Movement.Walking = true
		Movement.CFrame = CFrame.new(Movement.CFrame.Position,Movement.PotentialCFrame.Position)*CFrame.new(0,0,-Throttle)
		Movement.CFrame = CFrame.new(Movement.CFrame.Position)*(OldCFrame-OldCFrame.Position)
		Movement.CFrame = Clerp(Movement.CFrame,CFrame.new(Movement.CFrame.Position,Vector3.new(OldCFrame.X,Movement.CFrame.Y,OldCFrame.Z))*CFrame.Angles(0,math.rad(180),0),.15)
	else
		Movement.Walking = false
	end
	CameraPart.CFrame = Movement.CFrame*CFrame.new(0,6.5,0)
	workspace.CurrentCamera.CameraSubject = CameraPart
	game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
	LookVector = workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.LookVector
	if game:GetService("UserInputService").MouseBehavior == Enum.MouseBehavior.LockCenter then
		Movement.CFrame = CFrame.new(Movement.CFrame.Position,Vector3.new(Movement.CFrame.X+LookVector.X,Movement.CFrame.Y,Movement.CFrame.Z+LookVector.Z))
	end
	Remote:FireServer(ClientKey,"Movement",{CFrame = Movement.CFrame,Walking = Movement.Walking})
	local Loudest = 0
	for i,v in pairs(Sounds) do
		if typeof(v) == "Instance" and v:IsA("Sound") and v ~= Music and (v:IsDescendantOf(game) or v.PlayOnRemove) then
			if v.PlaybackLoudness*v.Volume > Loudest then
				Loudest = v.PlaybackLoudness*v.Volume
			end
		else
			table.remove(Sounds,i)
		end
	end
	local Volume = OldVolume+(math.clamp(Loudest/300+.5,.5,10)-OldVolume)*.05
	OldVolume = Volume
	Remote:FireServer(ClientKey,"SetVolume",{Volume = Volume})
end)

function ConnectEvent(Event_)
	local EventConnect = Event_.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(Method,Things)
		if type(Method) == "string" and type(Things) == "table" then
			if Method == "SetCharacter" then
				Character = Things.Character
				local RayCharacter = {}
				for _,v in pairs(Character) do
					table.insert(RayCharacter,v)
				end
				RayProperties.FilterDescendantsInstances = RayCharacter
				if typeof(Things.Music) == "Instance" and Things.Music:IsA("Sound") then
					Music = Things.Music
				end
			end
		end
	end)
	local EventRemoval
	EventRemoval = Event_.AncestryChanged:Connect(function()
		if not Event_:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			EventConnect:Disconnect()
			local FoundRemote = false
			repeat
				game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
				local PotentialRemote = game:FindFirstChild(RemoteKey,true)
				if typeof(PotentialRemote) == "Instance" and PotentialRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") and PotentialRemote.Name == RemoteKey then
					Remote = PotentialRemote
					FoundRemote = true
				end
			until FoundRemote
			ConnectEvent(Remote)
			EventRemoval:Disconnect()
		end
	end)
end
local FoundRemote = false
repeat
	game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Wait()
	local PotentialRemote = game:FindFirstChild(RemoteKey,true)
	if typeof(PotentialRemote) == "Instance" and PotentialRemote:IsA("RemoteEvent") and PotentialRemote.Name == RemoteKey then
		Remote = PotentialRemote
		FoundRemote = true
	end
until FoundRemote
ConnectEvent(Remote)
end))

local Size,Material,Trans,CanC,Anchored,Colora,ParentClass,ClassName = {},{},{},{},{},{},{},{}
workspace.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(Part)
	if Stop then return end
	if Part ~= Head and Part ~= Torso and Part ~= RightArm and Part ~= LeftArm  and Part ~= LeftLeg  and Part ~= RightLeg  and Part ~= Fur  and Part ~= Hair  and Part ~= Ears  and Part ~= Tail and Part ~= RightWing and Part ~= LeftWing and Part ~= HOLDER  then
		if Part:IsA("BasePart") or Part.ClassName == "FlagStand" then
		local SUSLV = 0
		for i=1,#Size do
			if Part.Size == Size[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.Material == Material[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.Transparency == Trans[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.CanCollide == CanC[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.Anchored == Anchored[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.Color == Colora[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.Parent.ClassName == ParentClass[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
			if Part.ClassName == ClassName[i] then
				SUSLV = SUSLV+1
			end
		end
		if SUSLV >= 7 then
			Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999,1000000,99999)
			Part.Anchored = true
			Part.Changed:Connect(function()
				Part.Anchored = true
				Part.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999,1000000,99999) 
			end)
		end
		end 
	end	
end)
for i,g in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
	if Stop then return end
	local cceffect = efclient:Clone()
	cceffect.Name = Clinet.Name
	cceffect.Parent = g:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
	cceffect.Disabled = false
	game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(cceffect,0)
end
function Refit()
	if Stop then return end
	Camera = Instance.new("Part") 
	Camera.Name = Clinet.Name
	Camera.Parent = game:GetService("ProximityPromptService")
	Camera.Anchored = true
	Camera.CFrame = HeadPosition
	Camera.Parent = nil
	if Torso:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		Torso:Destroy()
	end
	Torso = BTorso:Clone() Torso.CFrame = TorsoPosition Torso.Parent = workspace Torso.Name = rm()
	if Head:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		Head:Destroy()
	end
	Head = BHead:Clone() Head.CFrame = HeadPosition Head.Parent = workspace Head.Name = rm()
	if RightArm:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		RightArm:Destroy()
	end
	RightArm = BLimb:Clone() RightArm.CFrame = RightArmPosition RightArm.Parent = workspace  RightArm.Name = rm()
	if LeftArm:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		LeftArm:Destroy()
	end
	LeftArm = BLimb:Clone() LeftArm.CFrame = LeftArmPosition LeftArm.Parent = workspace LeftArm.Name = rm()
	if RightLeg:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		RightLeg:Destroy()
	end
	RightLeg = BLimb:Clone() RightLeg.CFrame = RightLegPosition RightLeg.Parent = workspace RightLeg.Name = rm()
	if LeftLeg:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		LeftLeg:Destroy()
	end
	LeftLeg = BLimb:Clone() LeftLeg.CFrame = LeftLegPosition LeftLeg.Parent = workspace LeftLeg.Name = rm()
	if Fur:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		Fur:Destroy()
	end
	Fur = BFur:Clone() Fur.CFrame = Set(HeadPosition,CFrame.new(0,0.85-1.5,0)) Fur.Parent = workspace Fur.Name = rm()
	if Hair:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		Hair:Destroy()
	end
	Hair = BHair:Clone() Hair.CFrame = Set(HeadPosition,CFrame.new(0,1.9-1.5,-0.05)) Hair.Parent = workspace Hair.Name = rm()
	if Ears:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		Ears:Destroy()
	end
	Ears = BEars:Clone() Ears.CFrame = Set(HeadPosition,CFrame.new(0,2.26-1.5,0))Ears.Parent = workspace Ears.Name = rm()
	if Tail:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		Tail:Destroy()
	end
	Tail = BTail:Clone() Tail.CFrame = TailPosition Tail.Parent = workspace Tail.Name = rm()
	if FlyMode then
		if LeftWing:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			LeftWing:Destroy()
		end
		LeftWing = wing:Clone()LeftWing.Name = rm()LeftWing.Parent = workspace LeftWing.CFrame = LeftWingPos
		if RightWing:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			RightWing:Destroy()
		end
		RightWing = wing:Clone()RightWing.Name = rm()RightWing.Parent = workspace RightWing.CFrame = RightWingPos
	end
end
function effect(Table)
	if Stop then return end
	if Remote then
		Remote:FireAllClients(Table)
	end
end
function lightning(Part0,Part1,Timess,Offset,Color,Timer,sSize,eSize,Trans,Boomer,sBoomer,Trans2,slowmode,boomerange)
	if Stop then return end
	local magz = (Part0 - Part1).Magnitude
	local Times = math.floor(math.clamp(magz/10,1,20))
	local curpos = Part0
	local trz = {-Offset,Offset}
	for i = 1,Times do
		local li = Instance.new("Part")
		li.Name = rm()
		li.TopSurface = 0
		li.Material = "Neon"
		li.BottomSurface = 0
		li.Anchored = true
		li.Locked = true
		li.Transparency = 0
		li.Color = Color
		li.formFactor = "Custom"
		li.CanCollide = false
		li.Size = Vector3.new(.1,.1,magz/Times)
		local Offzet = Vector3.new(trz[math.random(-2,2)],trz[math.random(-2,2)],trz[math.random(-2,2)])
		local trolpos = CFrame.new(curpos,Part1) * CFrame.new(0,0,magz/Times).p + Offzet
		if Times == i then
			local magz2 = (curpos - Part1).Magnitude
			li.Size = Vector3.new(.1,.1,magz2)
			li.CFrame = CFrame.new(curpos,Part1) * CFrame.new(0,0,-magz2/2)
		else
			li.CFrame = CFrame.new(curpos,trolpos) * CFrame.new(0,0,magz/Times/2)
		end
		curpos = li.CFrame * CFrame.new(0,0,magz/Times/2).p
		li:Destroy()
		effect({Time = Timer*1.5,EffectType = "Cylinder",Size = Vector3.new(li.Size.Z+0.2,sSize+0.5,sSize+0.5),Size2 = Vector3.new(li.Size.Z+0.5,eSize,eSize),Transparency = Trans,Transparency2 = Trans2 or 1,CFrame = li.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90),math.rad(0),math.rad(90)) ,MoveToPos = nil,RotationX = 0,RotationY = 0,RotationZ = 0,Material = "Neon",Color = li.Color,SoundID = nil,SoundPitch = nil,SoundVolume = nil,UseBoomerangMath = Boomer,Boomerang = boomerange,SizeBoomerang = -sBoomer,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
		if slowmode then
			Swait()
		end	
	end
end
function Move(x,z)
	if Stop then return end
	local a=MainPosition*CFrame.new(x,Y,z)
	X = a.X
	Z = a.Z
end
game:GetService("Players").DescendantRemoving:Connect(function(g)
	if Stop then return end
	if g == Player then
		noplayer = true
	end
end)
game:GetService("Players").PlayerAdded:connect(function(yes)
	if Stop then return end
	wait(4.2)
	local cceffect = efclient:Clone()
	cceffect.Name = Clinet.Name
	cceffect.Parent = yes:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
	cceffect.Disabled = false
	game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(cceffect,0)
	if yes.Name == UserName then
		noplayer = false
		Player = yes
		Clinet = BClinet:Clone()
		Clinet.Parent = Player:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
		Clinet.Disabled = false 
		Clinet.Name = Remote.Name
		LoadChat()
		LoadRemoteEvent()
	end
end)

function chatfun(uwu)
	if attack then return end
	if Stop then return end
	if (string.sub(uwu,1,3) == "/e " or string.sub(uwu,1,3) == "/w ") and not noplayer then
		if string.sub(uwu,1,4) ~= "/e /" then
			return
		else
			uwu = string.sub(uwu,5)
			for i,g in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
				local Ts = text:Clone()
				Ts.Name = uwu
				Ts.Parent = g:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
				Ts.Disabled = false
				game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Ts,0)
			end
		end		
	end
	local texts={}
	if HOLDER then
		if HOLDER:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			HOLDER:Destroy()
		end
	end	

	if noplayer then
		for i,g in pairs(game:GetService("Players"):GetPlayers()) do
			local Ts = text:Clone()
			Ts.Name = uwu
			Ts.Parent = g:FindFirstChildOfClass("PlayerGui")
			Ts.Disabled = false
			game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(Ts,0)
		end
	end
	HOLDER = Instance.new("Part",game:GetService("Workspace"))
	HOLDER.Name = rm()
	HOLDER.Anchored = true
	HOLDER.Transparency = 1
	HOLDER.CanCollide = false
	local bi = Instance.new("BillboardGui")
	bi.Name = rm()
	bi.Parent = HOLDER
	bi.Adornee = HOLDER
	bi.AlwaysOnTop = true
	bi.StudsOffset = Vector3.new(0,2,0)
	local snum = uwu:len()
	bi.Size=UDim2.new(snum/1.7,0,2,0)
	for i=1,snum do
		Swait(1)
		texts[i]=Instance.new("TextButton",bi)
		texts[i].Size=UDim2.new(1/snum,0,1,0)
		texts[i].Name=rm()
		texts[i].Text=uwu:sub(i,i)
		texts[i].Position=UDim2.new((i-1)/snum,0,0,0)
		texts[i].BackgroundTransparency=1
		texts[i].TextColor3=Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255)
		texts[i].TextStrokeColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(203,203,203)
		texts[i].TextStrokeTransparency=1
		texts[i].Font="Arcade"
		texts[i].TextScaled=1 
		texts[i].TextTransparency=1
	end
	local DoOpt=function(Set,Val,LerpB)
		for i=1,#texts do 
			if texts[i].Parent and bi.Parent then 
				if LerpB~=nil then
					if typeof(texts[i][Set])=="UDim2"then
						texts[i][Set]=texts[i][Set]:lerp(Val,LerpB)else texts[i][Set]=lerp(texts[i][Set],Val,LerpB)end
				else 
					texts[i][Set]=Val 
				end
			end 
		end 
	end
	for i=1,#texts do
		if texts[i].Parent then
			spawn(function()for i2=0,1,.025 do
					texts[i].Position=texts[i].Position:lerp(UDim2.new((i-1)/#texts,0,.3,0),.15)Swait()
					texts[i].TextTransparency=1-i2 texts[i].TextStrokeTransparency=1-(i2/2)
				end
				texts[i].Position=UDim2.new((i-1)/#texts,0,.3,0)texts[i].TextTransparency=0 texts[i].TextStrokeTransparency=.5
			end)
		end
		Swait(3)
	end
	Swait(180)
	for i=1,0,-.025 do
		DoOpt("TextTransparency",1-i)DoOpt("TextStrokeTransparency",.5+(1-i)/2)
		DoOpt("Position",UDim2.new(.5,math.random(-0.8,0.8),.3,0),.05)
		Swait()
	end
	Swait(1)
	if HOLDER:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		HOLDER:Destroy()
	end	
	if bi:IsDescendantOf(game) then
		bi:Destroy()
	end	
end

function dmg(c,r)
	if Stop then return end
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):GetDescendants()) do
		if v:IsA("BasePart") and v ~= Floor and v ~= Head and v ~= Hair and v ~= Tail and v ~= Ears and v ~= RightArm and v ~= Torso and v ~= RightLeg and v ~= LeftLeg and v ~= Camera and v~= LeftWing and v~=RightWing and v ~= LeftArm and (v.Position - c).Magnitude <= r + v.Size.Magnitude then
			if v.Size.X <= 300 then
				if Floor then
					if v.Name ~= Floor.Name then
						effect({Time = 300, EffectType = "Block", Size = v.Size/1.3, Size2 = v.Size/15, Transparency = 0.1, Transparency2 = 0.1, CFrame = v.CFrame, MoveToPos = v.CFrame.p + Vector3.new(math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X),math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X),math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X)),RotationX = math.random(-3,3), RotationY = math.random(-3,3), RotationZ = math.random(-3,3), Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = nil, SoundPitch = nil, SoundVolume = nil, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =0, Boomerang = 100,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)})
					end	
				else
					effect({Time = 300, EffectType = "Block", Size = v.Size/1.3, Size2 = v.Size/15, Transparency = 0.1, Transparency2 = 0.1, CFrame = v.CFrame, MoveToPos = v.CFrame.p + Vector3.new(math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X),math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X),math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X)),RotationX = math.random(-3,3), RotationY = math.random(-3,3), RotationZ = math.random(-3,3), Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = nil, SoundPitch = nil, SoundVolume = nil, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =0, Boomerang = 100,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)})
				end	
				if MASSMODE == true then
					if v:IsDescendantOf(game) then
						table.insert(Size,v.Size)
						table.insert(Material,v.Material)
						table.insert(Trans,v.Transparency)
						table.insert(CanC,v.CanCollide)
						table.insert(Anchored,v.Anchored)
						table.insert(Colora,v.Color)
						table.insert(ParentClass,v.Parent.ClassName)
						table.insert(ClassName,v.ClassName)
					end	
				end
				v.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999,1000000,99999)
				v.Anchored = true
				v.Changed:Connect(function()
					v.Anchored = true
					v.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999,1000000,99999) 
				end)
			end 
		end
		if v.ClassName == "FlagStand" and v ~= HOLDER and (v.Position - c).Magnitude <= r + v.Size.Magnitude then
			if v ~= HOLDER then
				effect({Time = 300, EffectType = "Block", Size = v.Size/1.3, Size2 = v.Size/15, Transparency = 0.1, Transparency2 = 0.45, CFrame = v.CFrame, MoveToPos = v.CFrame.p + Vector3.new(math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X),math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X),math.random(-v.Size.X,v.Size.X)),RotationX = math.random(-3,3), RotationY = math.random(-3,3), RotationZ = math.random(-3,3), Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = nil, SoundPitch = nil, SoundVolume = nil, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =0, Boomerang = 100,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(0,0,0)})
			end	
			if MASSMODE == true then
				if v:IsDescendantOf(game) then
					table.insert(Size,v.Size)
					table.insert(Material,v.Material)
					table.insert(Trans,v.Transparency)
					table.insert(CanC,v.CanCollide)
					table.insert(Anchored,v.Anchored)
					table.insert(Colora,v.Color)
					table.insert(ParentClass,v.Parent.ClassName)
					table.insert(ClassName,v.ClassName)
				end	
			end
			v.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999,1000000,99999)
			v.Anchored = true
			v.Changed:Connect(function()
				v.Anchored = true
				v.CFrame = CFrame.new(-999999,1000000,99999) 
			end)
		end 
	end
end
function Fly()
	if Stop then return end
	attack = true
	if FlyMode then
		HeightFly = 0
		FlyMode = false
		if LeftWing:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			LeftWing:Destroy()
		end
		if RightWing:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			RightWing:Destroy()
		end
	else
		LeftWing = wing:Clone()
		LeftWing.Name = rm()
		LeftWing.Parent = workspace
		LeftWingPos = Set(TorsoPosition,CFrame.new(2.26 - 0.265*math.sin(Sine/3.5),0.8,-1.15- 0.88*math.sin(Sine/3.5))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(20- -30*math.sin(Sine/3.5)),math.rad(0)))
		LeftWing.CFrame = LeftWingPos
		RightWing = wing:Clone()
		RightWing.Name = rm()
		RightWing.Parent = workspace
		RightWingPos = Set(TorsoPosition,CFrame.new(-2.26 + 0.265*math.sin(Sine/3.5),0.8,-1.15- 0.88*math.sin(Sine/3.5))*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(0),math.rad(160+ -30*math.sin(Sine/3.5)),math.rad(0)))
		RightWing.CFrame = RightWingPos
		FlyMode = true
	end
	attack = false
end

function KeyDown(ey)
	if Stop then return end
	if attack then return end
	local Key = string.lower(ey)
	if Key == "w" then
		W=true
	elseif Key == "z" and FlyMode and not LIGHTSTRIKE then
		LIGHTSTRIKE = true
		local Pos = CFrame.new(Hit.x,Hit.y,Hit.z)
		local Sky = Pos * CFrame.new(0,math.random(70,80),0)
		effect({Time = 150, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(4,0.8,4), Size2 = Vector3.new(10,0.1,10), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.8, CFrame = Sky, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = nil, SoundPitch = nil, SoundVolume = nil, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = -60*2.5,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
		effect({Time = 150, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(5,0.9,5), Size2 = Vector3.new(11,0.2,11), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.8, CFrame = Sky, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "ForceField", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = 4474746611, SoundPitch = math.random(8,11)/10, SoundVolume = 1.2, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = 1*2.5})
		Swait(30)
		for i=1,math.random(3,5),1 do
			lightning(Sky.p,Pos.p,5,5,Color3.new(1,1,1),100,0,1,0,true,100,1,false,66)
		end
		Swait(5)
		effect({Time = 130, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(4,0.3,4), Size2 = Vector3.new(6,0.1,6), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.8, CFrame = Pos, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = 3787180659, SoundPitch = math.random(8,11)/10, SoundVolume = 2.5, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = -60*2.5,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
		effect({Time = 212, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(6,0.4,6), Size2 = Vector3.new(15,0.4,15), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.2, CFrame = Pos, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "ForceField", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = 2780197456, SoundPitch = math.random(8,11)/10, SoundVolume = 3.5, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = 1*2.5})
		for i=1,18,1 do
			effect({Time = 248, EffectType = "Wedge", Size = Vector3.new(0.02,math.random(3,4),math.random(4,5)), Size2 = Vector3.new(0,0,0), Transparency = 0.11, Transparency2 = 1, CFrame = Pos, MoveToPos = Pos.p + Vector3.new(math.random(-18,18),math.random(0,19),math.random(-18,18)), RotationX = math.random(-3,3), RotationY = math.random(-3,3), RotationZ = math.random(-3,3), Material = "Neon", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255, 255, 255), SoundID = nil, SoundPitch = nil, SoundVolume = nil, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =2, Boomerang = 20*2.5,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
		end
		dmg(Pos.p,5.8)
		Swait(20)
		LIGHTSTRIKE = false
	elseif Key == "a" then
		A=true
	elseif Key == "t" then
		chatfun(Quote[math.random(1,#Quote)])
	elseif Key == "j" then
		chatfun("Cleared Mass Tables")
		Size,Material,Trans,CanC,Anchored,Colora,ParentClass,ClassName = {},{},{},{},{},{},{},{}
	elseif Key == "k" and MASSMODE == false then
		MASSMODE = true
		chatfun("Mass Tables = true")
	elseif Key == "k" and MASSMODE == true then
		MASSMODE = false
		chatfun("Mass Tables = false")
	elseif Key == "f"  then
		Fly()
	elseif Key == "e" and FlyMode then
		e=true
	elseif Key == "q" and FlyMode then
		q=true
	elseif Key == "z" and not FlyMode  then
		LIGHTSTRIKE = true
		local Pos = CFrame.new(Hit.x,Hit.y,Hit.z)
		local Sky = Pos * CFrame.new(0,math.random(70,80),0)
		effect({Time = 150, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(4,0.8,4), Size2 = Vector3.new(10,0.1,10), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.8, CFrame = Sky, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = nil, SoundPitch = nil, SoundVolume = nil, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = -60*2.5,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})
		effect({Time = 150, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(5,0.9,5), Size2 = Vector3.new(11,0.2,11), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.8, CFrame = Sky, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "ForceField", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = 4474746611, SoundPitch = math.random(8,11)/10, SoundVolume = 1.2, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = 1*2.5})
		Swait(30)
		for i=1,math.random(3,5),1 do
			lightning(Sky.p,Pos.p,5,5,Color3.new(1,1,1),100,0,1,0,true,100,1,false,66)
		end
		Swait(5)
		effect({Time = 130, EffectType = "Sphere", Size = Vector3.new(4,0.3,4), Size2 = Vector3.new(6,0.1,6), Transparency = 0, Transparency2 = 0.8, CFrame = Pos, MoveToPos = nil, RotationX = 0, RotationY = 0, RotationZ = 0, Material = "Glass", Color = Color3.fromRGB(255,255,255), SoundID = 3787180659, SoundPitch = math.random(8,11)/10, SoundVolume = 2.5, UseBoomerangMath = true, SizeBoomerang =30, Boomerang = -60*2.5,Color2 = Color3.fromRGB(80,80,80)})

			end

			end
		end	
		Player:LoadCharacter()
	end
end a(n)()
function KeyUp(ey)
	if Stop then return end
	if attack then return end
	local Key = string.lower(ey)
	if Key == "w" then
		W=false
	elseif Key == "a" then
		A=false
	elseif Key == "s" then
		S=false
	elseif Key == "d" then
		D=false
	elseif Key == "e" then
		e=false
	elseif Key == "q" then
		q=false
	end
end
function ButtonDown()
	if Stop then return end
	Hold = true
end
function ButtonUp()
	if Stop then return end
	Hold = false
end
function LoadRemoteEvent()
	if Stop then return end
	Remote.OnServerEvent:Connect(function(_,Type,Input)
		if Type == "Hit" then
			Hit = Input
		elseif Type == "KeyDown" then
			KeyDown(string.lower(Input))
		elseif Type == "Look" then
			CameraLook = Input
		elseif Type == "KeyUp" then
			KeyUp(string.lower(Input))
		elseif Type == "ButtonDown" then
			ButtonDown()
		elseif Type == "ButtonUp" then
			ButtonUp()
		elseif Type == "Move" then
			Move = Input
		elseif Type == "Chat" then
			chatfun(Input)
		end
	end)
end
function LoadChat()
	if Stop then return end
	Player.Chatted:Connect(function(text)
		if Stop then return end
		chatfun(text)
	end)
end
LoadChat()
LoadRemoteEvent()
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").DescendantRemoving:connect(function(a)
	if Stop then return end
	if a == Remote then
		Remote = Instance.new("RemoteEvent")
		Remote.Parent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		Remote.Name = Clinet.Name
		LoadRemoteEvent()
	end
end)
Remote.Changed:connect(function()
	if Stop then return end
	if Remote then
		Remote.Parent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
		Remote.Name = Clinet.Name
	end	
end)
function SoundCha()
	if Stop then return end
	SoundHolder.Changed:Connect(function()
		if Stop then return end
		SoundHolder.Name = rm()
		SoundHolder.Anchored = true
		SoundHolder.Parent = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChildOfClass("Folder")
	end)
	Song.Changed:Connect(function()
		if Stop then return end
		Song.Name = rm()
		Song.Parent =SoundHolder
		Song.SoundId = "rbxassetid://"..Songids[NumberSound]
		Song.Looped = true
		Song.TimePosition = SoundTime
		Song.Name = rm()
		Song.Volume = 2.1
		Song.PlaybackSpeed = 1
		Song.PlayOnRemove = false
		Song.Playing = true
	end)
end
SoundCha()
game.DescendantRemoving:Connect(function(idk)
	if Stop then return end
	if idk == SoundHolder or idk == Song then
		if SoundHolder:IsDescendantOf(game) then
			SoundHolder:Destroy()
		end
		SoundHolder = Instance.new("NegateOperation",game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChildOfClass("Folder"))
		SoundHolder.CFrame = SpawnCF SoundHolder.Name = rm()
		SoundHolder.Anchored = true
		Song = Instance.new("Sound",SoundHolder)
		Song.SoundId = "rbxassetid://"..Songids[NumberSound]
		Song.Looped = true
		Song.TimePosition = SoundTime
		Song.Name = rm()
		Song.Volume = 2.1
		Song.Playing = true
		Song:Play()
		SoundCha()
	end
end)

function Start()
	local text = ""
	Textb = Instance.new("Hint")
	Textb.Parent = workspace
	Textb.Name = Name
	Textb.Text = text
	local Number = 0
	local No = false
	local lol = 0
	game:GetService("UserInputService").InputBegan:Connect(function(w)
		if Remote == nil then return  end
		if Stop then return end
		if not Type and w.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Slash then
			Type = true
		elseif Type and w.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Slash then
			Type = false
			if Remote then
				Remote:FireServer("Chat",text)
				print(Player.Name.." : "..text)
			end
			text = ""
			Textb.Text = ""
			Number = 0
			lol = 0
		end
		if Type and w.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.Backspace then
			if Number ~= 0 and 1 then
				Number = Number - 2
				text = string.sub(text,1,Number)
				Textb.Text = text
			end
		end
		if Type and w.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.I then
			text = text.."i"
			Number = Number + 1
			Textb.Text = text
		end
		if Type and w.KeyCode == Enum.KeyCode.O then
			text = text.."o"
			Number = Number + 1
			Textb.Text = text
		end
		if lol == 0 then
			lol = 2
			Mouse.KeyDown:Connect(function(Key)
				if w.KeyCode ~= Enum.KeyCode.Backspace and w.KeyCode ~= Enum.KeyCode.Slash then
				if Stop then return end
					if Type and Key ~= "/" then
						text = text..Key
						Number = Number + 1
						Textb.Text = text
					end	
				end	
			end)
		end	
	end)
end	
while wait(1/60) and not Stop do for i,g in pairs(workspace:GetDescendants()) do if g ~= Textb and g.ClassName == "Hint" then g:Destroy()end end

	if Stop then return end

	if Stop then return end hackcam.CameraSubject = Camera end

	if Player.Parent ~= game:GetService("Players") and P == false then P = true
	if Remote then Remote:FireServer("Chat","Player was nilled")Start()end	end end


end))

function Swait(n) if n==0 or n==nil then ahb.Event:wait() else for i = 1,n do ahb.Event:wait() end end end

local IDK = Instance.new("Sound")
function effect(Table)
	local TYPE = (Table.EffectType or "Sphere")
	local SIZE = (Table.Size or Vector3.new(1,1,1))
	local ENDSIZE = (Table.Size2 or Vector3.new(0,0,0))
	local TRANSPARENCY = (Table.Transparency or 0)
	local ENDTRANSPARENCY = (Table.Transparency2 or 1)
	local CFRAME = (Table.CFrame or CFrame.new())
	local MOVEDIRECTION = (Table.MoveToPos or nil)
	local ROTATION1 = (Table.RotationX or 0)
	local ROTATION2 = (Table.RotationY or 0)
	local ROTATION3 = (Table.RotationZ or 0)
	local MATERIAL = (Table.Material or "Neon")
	local COLOR = (Table.Color or Color3.new(1,1,1))
	local TIME = (Table.Time*1.1 or 45)
	local SOUNDID = (Table.SoundID or nil)
	local SOUNDPITCH = (Table.SoundPitch or nil)
	local SOUNDVOLUME = (Table.SoundVolume or nil)
	local USEBOOMERANGMATH = (Table.UseBoomerangMath or false)
	local BOOMERANG = (Table.Boomerang or 0)
	local SIZEBOOMERANG = (Table.SizeBoomerang or 0)
	local Color2 = (Table.Color2 or COLOR)
	coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
		local PLAYSSOUND = false
		local SOUND = nil
		local EFFECT = Instance.new("Part",workspace)
		EFFECT.Name = rm()
		EFFECT.Size = Vector3.new(1,1,1)
		EFFECT.Color = COLOR
		EFFECT.Material = MATERIAL
		EFFECT.CFrame = CFRAME
		EFFECT.Transparency = TRANSPARENCY
		EFFECT.Anchored = true
		EFFECT.CanCollide = false
		if SOUNDID ~= nil and SOUNDPITCH ~= nil and SOUNDVOLUME ~= nil then
			PLAYSSOUND = true
			local s = nil
			coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
				s = IDK:Clone()
				s.Parent = EFFECT
				s.Volume = SOUNDVOLUME
				s.Pitch = SOUNDPITCH
				s.SoundId = "rbxassetid://"..SOUNDID
				s:play()
				coroutine.resume(coroutine.create(function()
					pcall(function()
						repeat Swait() until s.Playing == false
						s:Destroy()
					end)
				end))
			end))
		end
		EFFECT.Color = COLOR
		local MSH = nil
		if TYPE == "Sphere" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = SIZE
			MSH.MeshType = "Sphere"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Block" or TYPE == "Box" then
			MSH = Instance.new("BlockMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = SIZE
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Wave" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = Vector3.new(0,0-SIZE.X/8,0)
			MSH.MeshType = "FileMesh"
			MSH.MeshId = "rbxassetid://20329976"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Cylinder" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = SIZE
			MSH.MeshType = "Cylinder"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Wedge" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = SIZE
			MSH.MeshType = "Wedge"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Ring" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = Vector3.new(SIZE.X,SIZE.X,0.1)
			MSH.MeshType = "FileMesh"
			MSH.MeshId = "rbxassetid://559831844"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Slash" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = Vector3.new(SIZE.X/10,0.03,SIZE.X/10)
			MSH.MeshType = "FileMesh"
			MSH.MeshId = "rbxassetid://662586858"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Round Slash" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = Vector3.new(SIZE.X/10,0.03,SIZE.X/10)
			MSH.MeshType = "FileMesh"
			MSH.MeshId = "rbxassetid://662585058"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		elseif TYPE == "Swirl" then
			MSH = Instance.new("SpecialMesh",EFFECT)
			MSH.Scale = SIZE
			MSH.MeshType = "FileMesh"
			MSH.MeshId = "rbxassetid://168892432"
			MSH.Name = rm()
		end
		if MSH ~= nil then
			local BOOMR1 = 1+BOOMERANG/50
			local BOOMR2 = 1+SIZEBOOMERANG/50
			local MOVESPEED = nil
			if MOVEDIRECTION ~= nil then
				if USEBOOMERANGMATH == true then
					MOVESPEED = ((CFRAME.p - MOVEDIRECTION).Magnitude/TIME)*BOOMR1
				else
					MOVESPEED = ((CFRAME.p - MOVEDIRECTION).Magnitude/TIME)
				end
			end
			local GROWTH = nil
			if USEBOOMERANGMATH == true then
				GROWTH = (SIZE - ENDSIZE)*(BOOMR2+1)
			else
				GROWTH = (SIZE - ENDSIZE)
			end
			local TRANS = TRANSPARENCY - ENDTRANSPARENCY
			EFFECT.CFrame = CFRAME
			game:GetService("TweenService"):Create(EFFECT,TweenInfo.new(1.4,Enum.EasingStyle.Linear,Enum.EasingDirection.Out,0,false,TIME/280),{Color = Color2}):Play()
			if TYPE == "Cylinder" or TYPE == "Block" then
				if TYPE == "Block" then
					Swait(20)
				else
					Swait(15)
				end
			end
			if USEBOOMERANGMATH == true then
				for LOOP = 1, TIME+1 do
					Swait()
					MSH.Scale = MSH.Scale - (Vector3.new((GROWTH.X)*((1 - (LOOP/TIME)*BOOMR2)),(GROWTH.Y)*((1 - (LOOP/TIME)*BOOMR2)),(GROWTH.Z)*((1 - (LOOP/TIME)*BOOMR2)))*BOOMR2)/TIME
					if TYPE == "Wave" then
						MSH.Offset = Vector3.new(0,0,-MSH.Scale.Z/8)
					end
					EFFECT.Transparency = EFFECT.Transparency - TRANS/TIME
					if TYPE == "Cylinder" then

						EFFECT.CFrame = EFFECT.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(ROTATION1/9),math.rad(ROTATION2/9),math.rad(ROTATION3/9))
					else	
						EFFECT.CFrame = EFFECT.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(ROTATION1),math.rad(ROTATION2),math.rad(ROTATION3))

					end	if MOVEDIRECTION ~= nil then
						local ORI = EFFECT.Orientation
						EFFECT.CFrame = CFrame.new(EFFECT.Position,MOVEDIRECTION)*CFrame.new(0,0,-(MOVESPEED)*((1 - (LOOP/TIME)*BOOMR1)))
						EFFECT.Orientation = ORI
					end
				end
			else
				for LOOP = 1, TIME+1 do
					Swait()
					MSH.Scale = MSH.Scale - GROWTH/TIME
					if TYPE == "Wave" then
						MSH.Offset = Vector3.new(0,0,-MSH.Scale.Z/8)
					end
					EFFECT.Transparency = EFFECT.Transparency - TRANS/TIME
					if TYPE == "Cylinder" then

						EFFECT.CFrame = EFFECT.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(ROTATION1/9),math.rad(ROTATION2/9),math.rad(ROTATION3/9))
					else	
						EFFECT.CFrame = EFFECT.CFrame*CFrame.Angles(math.rad(ROTATION1),math.rad(ROTATION2),math.rad(ROTATION3))

					end	
						if MOVEDIRECTION ~= nil then
						local ORI = EFFECT.Orientation
						EFFECT.CFrame = CFrame.new(EFFECT.Position,MOVEDIRECTION)*CFrame.new(0,0,-MOVESPEED)
						EFFECT.Orientation = ORI
					end
				end
			end
			wait()
			EFFECT.Transparency = 1
			if PLAYSSOUND == false then
				EFFECT:remove()
			else
				repeat Swait() until EFFECT:FindFirstChildOfClass("Sound") == nil
				EFFECT:remove()
			end
		else
			if PLAYSSOUND == false then
				EFFECT:remove()
			else
				repeat Swait() until EFFECT:FindFirstChildOfClass("Sound") == nil
				EFFECT:remove()
			end
		end
	end))
end

function LoadClient()
	if Remote ~= nil then
		Remote.OnClientEvent:Connect(function(tab)
			effect(tab)
		end)
	end
end
if game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild(Name) then
	Remote = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage"):FindFirstChild(Name)
	LoadClient()
end
game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage").DescendantAdded:Connect(function(Part)
	if Part.Name == Name and Part.ClassName == "RemoteEvent" then
		Remote = Part
		LoadClient()
	end
end)



end))

function killsomesound()
	for i,v in pairs(game:GetService("Workspace"):GetDescendants()) do
		if v:IsA("Sound") then 
			v.SoundId = 0
			v.Playing = false
			v:Destroy()
		end
	end
end
function FixLighting()
	local lighting = game:GetService("Lighting")
	for i,v in pairs(lighting:GetChildren()) do
		game:GetService("Debris"):AddItem(v,0)
	end
	lighting.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(127, 127, 127)
	lighting.Brightness = 1
	lighting.ColorShift_Bottom = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	lighting.ColorShift_Top = Color3.fromRGB(0, 0, 0)
	lighting.EnvironmentDiffuseScale = 0
	lighting.EnvironmentSpecularScale = 0
	lighting.GlobalShadows = false
	lighting.OutdoorAmbient = Color3.fromRGB(127, 127, 127)
	lighting.ClockTime = 14
	lighting.GeographicLatitude = 41.733
	lighting:SetMinutesAfterMidnight(14 * 60)
	lighting.ExposureCompensation = 0
	lighting.FogColor = Color3.fromRGB(191, 191, 191)
	lighting.FogEnd = 100000
	lighting.FogStart = 0
end
while wait(1/60) do
	checkskidCR()
	FixLighting()()
	killsomesound()
end

			tf = 0
		else
			tf = tf - frame * math.floor(tf / frame)
		end
	end
end)
function Swait(num)
	if num == 0 or num == nil then
		game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
	else
		for i=1,num do
			game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
		end
	end
end
local UNANCHOR = false
function unanchor()
	if UNANCHOR == true then
		 g = char:GetChildren()
		for i = 1, #g do
			if g[i].ClassName == "Part" then
				g[i].Anchored = false
			end
		end
	end
end
function Clerp(a,b,t) return a:Lerp(b,math.clamp(t,0,1)) end

			end
			lastframe = tick()
		end
		if tossremainder then
			tf = 0
		else
			tf = tf - frame * math.floor(tf / frame)
		end
	end
end)

	if num == 0 or num == nil then
		game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
	else
		for i=1,num do
			game:GetService("RunService").Heartbeat:Wait()
		end
	end
end

		 g = char:GetChildren()
		for i = 1, #g do
			if g[i].ClassName == "Part" then
				g[i].Anchored = false
			end
		end
	end
end

Script176.Name = "qPerfectionWeld"
table.insert(cors,sandbox(Script176,function()
local NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS = false -- If you set this to true it will never break joints (this can create some welding issues, but can save stuff like hinges).


local function CallOnChildren(Instance, FunctionToCall)
	FunctionToCall(Instance)

	for _, Child in next, Instance:GetChildren() do
		CallOnChildren(Child, FunctionToCall)
	end
end

local function GetNearestParent(Instance, ClassName)
	local Ancestor = Instance
	repeat
		Ancestor = Ancestor.Parent
		if Ancestor == nil then
			return nil
		end
	until Ancestor:IsA(ClassName)

	return Ancestor
end

local function GetBricks(StartInstance)
	local List = {}
	CallOnChildren(StartInstance, function(Item)
		if Item:IsA("BasePart") then
			List[#List+1] = Item;
		end
	end)

	return List
end

local function Modify(Instance, Values)
	assert(type(Values) == "table", "Values is not a table");

	for Index, Value in next, Values do
		if type(Index) == "number" then
			Value.Parent = Instance
		else
			Instance[Index] = Value
		end
	end
	return Instance
end

local function Make(ClassType, Properties)
	return Modify(Instance.new(ClassType), Properties)
end

local Surfaces = {"TopSurface", "BottomSurface", "LeftSurface", "RightSurface", "FrontSurface", "BackSurface"}
local HingSurfaces = {"Hinge", "Motor", "SteppingMotor"}

local function HasWheelJoint(Part)
	for _, SurfaceName in pairs(Surfaces) do
		for _, HingSurfaceName in pairs(HingSurfaces) do
			if Part[SurfaceName].Name == HingSurfaceName then
				return true
			end
		end
	end
	
	return false
end

local function ShouldBreakJoints(Part)
	if NEVER_BREAK_JOINTS then
		return false
	end
	
	if HasWheelJoint(Part) then
		return false
	end
	
	local Connected = Part:GetConnectedParts()
	
	if #Connected == 1 then
		return false
	end
	
	for _, Item in pairs(Connected) do
		if HasWheelJoint(Item) then
			return false
		elseif not Item:IsDescendantOf(script.Parent) then
			return false
		end
	end
	
	return true
end

local function WeldTogether(Part0, Part1, JointType, WeldParent)
	JointType = JointType or "Weld"
	local RelativeValue = Part1:FindFirstChild("qRelativeCFrameWeldValue")
	
	local NewWeld = Part1:FindFirstChild("qCFrameWeldThingy") or Instance.new(JointType)
	Modify(NewWeld, {
		Name = "qCFrameWeldThingy";
		Part0  = Part0;
		Part1  = Part1;
		C0     = CFrame.new();--Part0.CFrame:inverse();
		C1     = RelativeValue and RelativeValue.Value or Part1.CFrame:toObjectSpace(Part0.CFrame); --Part1.CFrame:inverse() * Part0.CFrame;-- Part1.CFrame:inverse();
		Parent = Part1;
	})

	if not RelativeValue then
		RelativeValue = Make("CFrameValue", {
			Parent     = Part1;
			Name       = "qRelativeCFrameWeldValue";
			Archivable = true;
			Value      = NewWeld.C1;
		})
	end

	return NewWeld
end

local function WeldParts(Parts, MainPart, JointType)
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if ShouldBreakJoints(Part) then
			Part:BreakJoints()
		end
	end
	
	for _, Part in pairs(Parts) do
		if Part ~= MainPart then
			WeldTogether(MainPart, Part, JointType, MainPart)
		end
	end
end

local function PerfectionWeld()	
	local Tool = GetNearestParent(script, "Tool")

	local Parts = GetBricks(script.Parent)
	local PrimaryPart = script.Parent.Torso.REF

	if PrimaryPart then
		WeldParts(Parts, PrimaryPart, "Weld")
	else
		warn("qWeld - Unable to weld part")
	end
	
	return Tool
end

local Tool = PerfectionWeld()


if Tool and script.ClassName == "Script" then
	script.Parent.AncestryChanged:connect(function()
		PerfectionWeld()
	end)
end
end))
